### ADR-0004 / SPEC §6.3 (T-EXEC-13c..13m + T-EXEC-03b/03c/07a/07b/16c/16d — CJS rejection matrix + cwd-isolation + Bash invocation contracts) — RESOLVED

SPEC §6.3 normatively requires that any CommonJS syntax (`require()`, `module.exports`, `exports.foo`) inside a loopx script (`.js` / `.ts` / `.tsx` / `.jsx`) **fails at execution time**. The existing implementation at `packages/loop-extender/src/loader-hook.ts` only forced ESM for `.js` files in `.loopx/`. For `.ts`, `.tsx`, and `.jsx` files, the implementation delegated to `tsx`'s loader, which under Node ultimately routes the source through `esbuild.transform({ format: "esm", loader: "ts"|"tsx"|"jsx" })`. esbuild's `format: "esm"` path detects CJS-style assignments and auto-wraps the body in a `__commonJS()` factory that exposes `module` and `exports` as function parameters — defeating the SPEC §6.3 rejection contract under Node+tsx for the `module.exports` and `exports.foo` branches across the three TS/JSX extensions (6 of 11 cases). Bun's parser independently rejects `module.exports` / `exports.foo` when `import` is present and the `--define require:null` flag rejects `require()`, so the rule already held under Bun.

Implementation (this iteration):

1. **`packages/loop-extender/package.json`**: added `esbuild: "^0.27.0"` as a runtime dependency (previously transitive via `tsx`).

2. **`packages/loop-extender/src/loader-hook.ts`**: extended the `.loopx/`-scoped force-ESM branch to handle `.ts` / `.tsx` / `.jsx` in addition to `.js`. For these extensions the hook now reads the source directly, transforms via `esbuild.transform(...)` with `loader: "ts"|"tsx"|"jsx"` and **deliberately omits the `format` option** (passing `format: "esm"` triggers esbuild's CJS-shim wrapper). With no format option, esbuild emits plain transformed JS (TS types stripped, JSX expanded to `React.createElement` calls per the existing JSX classic-transform contract from execution.ts) preserving the user's CJS references intact. The hook returns the transformed source as `format: "module"` with `shortCircuit: true`, so Node evaluates it as a true ES module — `module`, `exports`, and `require` are not in scope, and any reference throws `ReferenceError` at evaluation time. Excludes `node_modules/` to avoid breaking workflow CJS dependencies.

Now-passing tests (this iteration) in `apps/tests/tests/e2e/execution.test.ts`:

- **T-EXEC-13c (.js + module.exports)**, **T-EXEC-13d (.js + exports.foo)** — `.js` cases (loader-hook already enforced ESM here).
- **T-EXEC-13e (.ts + require())**, **T-EXEC-13f (.jsx + require())**, **T-EXEC-13g (.tsx + require())** — `require()` cases on TS/JSX (already enforced via auto-injected `.loopx/package.json {"type":"module"}` from `bin-path.ts`).
- **T-EXEC-13h (.ts + module.exports)**, **T-EXEC-13i (.jsx + module.exports)**, **T-EXEC-13j (.tsx + module.exports)** — newly enforced by the loader-hook fix; previously silently succeeded under Node+tsx.
- **T-EXEC-13k (.ts + exports.foo)**, **T-EXEC-13l (.jsx + exports.foo)**, **T-EXEC-13m (.tsx + exports.foo)** — newly enforced by the loader-hook fix; previously silently succeeded under Node+tsx.
- **T-EXEC-03b (Bash `cd` does not leak intra-workflow goto)**, **T-EXEC-03c (Bash `cd` does not leak across loop reset)** — pin SPEC §6.1 "later spawns always start at project-root cwd" on the no-goto loop-reset path in addition to the goto path. Test-only iteration; the existing `executeScript` call site in `loop.ts` already passes `cwd = projectRoot` for every spawn.
- **T-EXEC-07a (.sh script without executable bit still runs)** — pins SPEC §6.2 "loopx invokes Bash scripts as `/bin/bash <script>`, so the executable bit is not required". Test-only iteration; `executeScript` calls `spawn("/bin/bash", [script.path], ...)`.
- **T-EXEC-07b (.sh scripts invoked via absolute `/bin/bash`, not PATH-resolved `bash`)** — pins SPEC §6.2 "Bash scripts are executed as child processes via `/bin/bash`". Fixture creates a fake `bash` shim in a throwaway dir, prepends it to `PATH`, asserts the real `/bin/bash` ran (real-bash marker exists, fake-bash sentinel does not). Test-only iteration; `executeScript` hardcodes `command = "/bin/bash"`.
- **T-EXEC-16c (`process.chdir()` does not leak intra-workflow goto)**, **T-EXEC-16d (`process.chdir()` does not leak across loop reset)** — JS/TS counterparts to T-EXEC-03b/03c on the goto + loop-reset paths. Test-only iteration; same `cwd = projectRoot` propagation in `executeScript` covers JS/TS spawns.

Test counts:
- **execution.test.ts: 79/79 PASS** (was 45/45, +34 new — 17 IDs × 2 runtimes for most, + 1-runtime tests for the small subset).
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions across **programmatic-api (398) + env-vars (96) + wfdir (40) + loop-state (96) + cli-basics (...) + discovery + output-parsing + module-resolution + exit-codes + version-check (1347 total across 10 e2e files), tmpdir.test.ts (569), signals (9), unit (143), harness (15), install.test.ts (385/386 — only T-INST-GLOBAL-01a still failing, pre-existing Bun global-install issue unrelated to this work)**.

The simpler "node_modules absence" assertion is insufficient because the TEST-SPEC mandates a shim-log assertion to catch a regression that runs `npm install` and immediately removes `node_modules/`.

### ADR-0004 §9.5 / §7.2 / §7.4 / §9.3 / §13 (T-API-57/57a/57b/57c/57d/57e/57f/57f2/57g/57g2/57h/57i + T-API-58/58a/58a2 — RunOptions.env runtime-rejection matrix + LOOPX_* silent-override) — RESOLVED

SPEC §9.5 contract: `RunOptions.env` is structurally validated as own-enumerable string-keyed string-to-string entries; loopx does NOT pre-validate names beyond shape (no POSIX `[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*` enforcement, no rejection of `=` / empty-string names). Runtime-level rejections (most reliably an embedded NUL byte in name or value) surface as child launch / spawn failures at spawn time per SPEC §7.2 / §9.3. SPEC §7.4 cleanup trigger list ("Child launch / spawn failure after tmpdir creation") + SPEC §9.3 ("Cleanup ordering is observable") together require that no `loopx-*` directory remains under the test-isolated TMPDIR parent after the spawn failure surfaces — cleanup runs before the generator throws or the promise rejects. SPEC §8.3 / §9.5 / §13: the five script-protocol-protected names (`LOOPX_BIN`, `LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR`, `LOOPX_TMPDIR`) supplied via `RunOptions.env` are silently overridden by protocol injection (no warning / notice on stderr); `LOOPX_DELEGATED` is startup-reserved only — NOT script-protocol-protected — so it propagates unchanged from `RunOptions.env` to the spawned child.

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/run.ts` (`snapshotEnv` at lines 72-103, `runInternal` env merging at lines 661-664: `{ ...mergeEnv(globalEnv, localEnv, inheritedEnv), ...(snap.env ?? {}) }`) and `packages/loop-extender/src/execution.ts` (protocol-var overlay at lines 179-185: `{ ...env, LOOPX_BIN, LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT, LOOPX_WORKFLOW, LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR, LOOPX_TMPDIR }`) ALREADY conformed: `snapshotEnv` rejects only the spec'd shape errors (null/array/function/non-object whole-env, non-string entry values) — NUL bytes / non-POSIX names / `=` / empty-string keys all pass shape validation and reach the runtime; the runtime's `child_process.spawn` env-validator surfaces them as spawn failures via the standard pre-iteration error path in `loop.ts`. Cleanup runs in `runLoop`'s try/finally (`packages/loop-extender/src/loop.ts:120-217`) before the spawn-failure error propagates out of the generator. The protocol-var overlay applies AFTER `snap.env` so `LOOPX_*` script-protocol names supplied by the user are replaced before the env reaches `child_process.spawn`. `LOOPX_DELEGATED` is not in the protocol-var overlay list, so it survives `snap.env` overlay and reaches the spawned child unchanged. Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **programmatic-api.test.ts: 552/552 PASS** (was 522, +30) — added 30 tests under two new `describe` blocks (24 in `SPEC: RunOptions.env Runtime Rejection`, 6 in `SPEC: RunOptions.env LOOPX_* Silent Override`):
  - **T-API-57 (runPromise + NUL value)** / **T-API-57a (runPromise + NUL key)**: bash fixture with marker. Driver awaits `runPromise("ralph", { env: ..., maxIterations: 1 })` under a test-isolated `TMPDIR` parent, captures rejection state. Asserts: (a) promise rejected with spawn-failure (not shape-validation) — error message does NOT match `/RunOptions\.env\[.*\] must be a string/` (load-bearing — the shape is valid, so a buggy implementation that rejected NUL at the shape gate would shift this), (b) workflow script did not run, (c) cleanup ran before rejection — no `loopx-*` directory remains under the isolated TMPDIR parent (load-bearing — a buggy implementation that surfaced spawn failure without running cleanup would leave residue and fail).
  - **T-API-57b (runPromise + "=" in key)** / **T-API-57c (runPromise + empty-string key)**: outcome is impl-defined (rejection OR resolution); asserts the failure surface is NEVER shape-validation. Catches buggy implementations that synthesized a stricter shape gate than SPEC §9.5 requires.
  - **T-API-57d (runPromise + maxIterations:0 + NUL value)** / **T-API-57e (runPromise + maxIterations:0 + NUL key)**: under maxIterations:0 no spawn occurs, so the runtime-rejection path cannot fire. Asserts: (a) promise resolves, (b) resolved value is `[]`, (c) no spawn-failure error on stderr, (d) no `LOOPX_TMPDIR` was created (per SPEC §7.1 step 6 / §7.4 — tmpdir is not created under maxIterations:0).
  - **T-API-57f / T-API-57f2 (run + maxIterations:0 + NUL value/key)**: generator-surface counterparts. First `next()` returns `{ done: true, value: undefined }` immediately; same no-spawn / no-tmpdir contract.
  - **T-API-57g / T-API-57g2 (runPromise + run + non-POSIX names)**: positive coverage — `1BAD` (digit-prefix) and `FOO-BAR` (dash-interior) reach the spawned child unchanged. SPEC §9.5: "loopx does not enforce the POSIX `[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*` name pattern". Catches an implementation that wrongly applied the SPEC §8.1 env-file POSIX key validator to `RunOptions.env` (which would silently drop these names and pass T-API-57/57a since those tests pivot on rejection outcomes). Marker file is JSON-encoded for round-trip fidelity (distinguish empty string from undefined).
  - **T-API-57h / T-API-57i (run + NUL value/key, maxIterations:1)**: generator-surface counterparts to T-API-57/57a. First `next()` rejects with spawn-failure; cleanup ran before throw — no `loopx-*` residue under isolated parent.
  - **T-API-58 (runPromise + LOOPX_WORKFLOW + CUSTOM peer)**: bash fixture observes both names. Driver passes `env: { LOOPX_WORKFLOW: "user-fake", CUSTOM: "user-val" }`. Asserts: (a) script observes `LOOPX_WORKFLOW="ralph"` (real, NOT user-fake — protocol-tier override applies), (b) `CUSTOM="user-val"` (non-protocol peer reached child — confirms override is per-name, not env-wide), (c) stderr matches NO `loopx_workflow.*(override|overrid|ignored|warning|notice)` regex (silent-override contract).
  - **T-API-58a / T-API-58a2 (runPromise + run + LOOPX_DELEGATED reaches child)**: bash fixture observes `LOOPX_DELEGATED`. Asserts: marker records `"user-supplied"` — `LOOPX_DELEGATED` is startup-reserved only on the loopx side and an ordinary non-protocol variable on the spawned-script side; the protocol-tier override that silently replaces script-protocol-protected `LOOPX_*` names does NOT apply to `LOOPX_DELEGATED`. Distinguishes the five script-protocol-protected names (T-API-51a/58) from the startup-only `LOOPX_DELEGATED`.
- Test infrastructure added (inlined in programmatic-api.test.ts): `makeIsolatedTmpdirParent(label)` creates a writable test-isolated TMPDIR parent under `os.tmpdir()` per TEST-SPEC §4.7 isolation guidance (concurrent test workers must not race on `/tmp`); `listLoopxEntries(parent)` filters implementation-internal helpers (nodepath-shim, bun-jsx, install-staging, test-parent itself) per AGENT.md / SPEC §7.4. Cleanup is registered for `afterEach`.
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions across tmpdir + signals (705/705 combined run), env-vars + wfdir (136/136), unit + harness (158/158), typecheck OK. Full programmatic-api.test.ts run: 552/552 in ~70s.

### ADR-0004 §9.5 / §9.1 (T-API-56/56a/56b/56c/56d/56e/56f/56g/56h/56i/56j — RunOptions.env filtering predicate) — RESOLVED

SPEC §9.5 contract: `RunOptions.env` is enumerated via the "own enumerable string-keyed properties" predicate. The predicate is a HARD filter applied BEFORE value-shape validation runs:
- Inherited (prototype-chain) properties are filtered (T-API-56, 56f, 56j).
- Symbol-keyed properties are filtered (T-API-56a, 56d).
- Non-enumerable string-keyed properties are filtered (T-API-56b, 56e).

The env-shape contract is structural-not-nominal — SPEC §9.5 rejects only `null`, arrays, and functions; any other non-null object qualifies regardless of prototype:
- Null-prototype object accepted; own entries reach child (T-API-56c).
- Class instance accepted; class fields reach child (T-API-56g).
- `Map` accepted as a shape but contributes zero entries (Map data lives in [[MapData]], not as own enumerable string-keyed properties — T-API-56h).

T-API-56j additionally pins the throwing-getter side-effect-suppression contract on the inherited axis (parameterized over both surfaces). T-API-56i is the run()-surface parity counterpart, parameterized across the 8 sub-rules to verify the generator surface routes env through the same filtering predicate.

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/run.ts` (`snapshotEnv` at lines 72-103) ALREADY conformed: `Object.keys(envRaw)` is exactly the SPEC-mandated predicate — returns own enumerable string-keyed properties only, does not walk the prototype chain (no `for ... in`), excludes symbols (built-in semantics), excludes non-enumerable. The structural-not-nominal contract is satisfied because `Object.keys` accepts any non-null object regardless of prototype (null-prototype, class instance, Map all work — Map's `Object.keys()` returns `[]` because Map's conceptual entries are not own enumerable string-keyed properties on the Map object itself). Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **programmatic-api.test.ts: 522/522 PASS** (was 482, +40) — added 40 tests (20 unique it() blocks × 2 runtimes) under a new `SPEC: RunOptions.env Filtering` describe block:
  - **T-API-56 (runPromise — inherited keys filtered)**: 1 ID × 2 runtimes = 2 tests. Drives `Object.create(proto)` with `proto = { INHERITED: "proto-val" }` and `e.OWN = "own-val"` on the child object. Asserts (a) script observes `OWN` with value `"own-val"`, (b) `INHERITED` is absent from child env (filtered before [[Get]] reached the inherited slot).
  - **T-API-56a (runPromise — symbol-keyed entries filtered)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. Bash fixture observes `OWN` and dumps all env var names to a marker; asserts no env var name matches `/^Symbol\(/` or equals `"SYM"` (load-bearing — common buggy stringifications would expose Symbol descriptions).
  - **T-API-56b (runPromise — non-enumerable filtered)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. Asserts `VISIBLE` reaches child, `HIDDEN` is absent.
  - **T-API-56c (runPromise — null-prototype env accepted)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. `Object.create(null)` with own entries; asserts no rejection AND own entries reach child. Catches a buggy implementation using `instanceof Object` (false for null-prototype) or calling `env.hasOwnProperty(...)` (TypeError on null-prototype — Object.prototype absent).
  - **T-API-56d (runPromise — symbol-keyed throwing getter)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. Symbol-keyed property has a throwing getter; asserts no rejection (slot never read, getter never fires) AND no error message about the getter on stderr.
  - **T-API-56e (runPromise — non-enumerable throwing getter)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. Same contract as T-API-56d but on the non-enumerable axis.
  - **T-API-56f (runPromise — inherited non-string-value)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. Inherited slot has non-string value (number 42); asserts no rejection (filtered BEFORE value validation — load-bearing — a buggy implementation enumerating via `for ... in` then validating values would surface the non-string and reject).
  - **T-API-56g (runPromise — class-instance env)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. `class Env { MYVAR = "from-class"; }` instance; asserts class-field reaches child (proves structural-not-nominal contract on non-plain-object axis).
  - **T-API-56h (runPromise — Map env contributes zero entries)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. `new Map([["MYVAR", "x"]])`; asserts no rejection (Map is non-null, non-array, non-function — accepted as shape) AND `MYVAR` is absent from child env (Map data lives in [[MapData]], not own-enumerable-string-keyed). Driver scrubs `MYVAR` from inherited env first to ensure observation can only come from the env option.
  - **T-API-56j (runPromise — inherited throwing getter)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. Inherited prototype slot has throwing getter; asserts no rejection (slot never read) AND no error message about the inherited getter on stderr.
  - **T-API-56j (run — inherited throwing getter)**: 1 × 2 = 2 tests. Generator-surface counterpart with distinct error message; asserts the lazy snapshot path also filters the inherited slot before any value-read.
  - **T-API-56i (a–h, run-surface 8 sub-variants)**: 8 × 2 = 16 tests. Each variant is a generator-surface counterpart of one runPromise() T-API-56* test, individually authored as separate `it()` blocks for clear failure attribution. Each asserts the same outcome as its runPromise counterpart but on the run() generator surface, verifying surface-parity for the SPEC §9.5 filtering, structural-shape-acceptance, and side-effect-suppression contracts.
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions — tmpdir + env-vars + wfdir + loop-state + execution (880/880 across 5 e2e files), signals (9/9), unit + harness (158/158), typecheck OK. Full programmatic-api.test.ts run: 522/522 in ~66s.

### ADR-0004 §8.3 / §9.5 / §13 / §7.2 (T-API-58b/58c/58d/58d2/58e/58e2 — RunOptions.env × NUL-protocol-name merge-order matrix on both API surfaces) — RESOLVED

SPEC §8.3 places loopx-injected protocol variables (`LOOPX_BIN`, `LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR`, `LOOPX_TMPDIR`) at the top precedence tier and silently overrides same-named values in any lower tier. SPEC §9.5 / §7.2 specify that runtime-level rejections of a child env entry (most reliably an embedded NUL byte in the value) "surface as child launch / spawn failures at spawn time" from "any env tier — the runtime does not distinguish tiers." T-API-58 / T-WFDIR-06 / T-WFDIR-07 / T-WFDIR-08 cover protocol-variable override against ordinary fake user values; T-API-57 / T-API-57a / T-ENV-26 / T-ENV-27 cover NUL-byte runtime rejection on **non**-protocol env entries. Neither set pinned down the **merge-order** interaction: when a lower tier supplies a `LOOPX_*` protocol variable with a NUL-containing value, the protocol-tier override must run BEFORE the merged env reaches the runtime, so the NUL value is silently replaced and no spawn failure occurs. The T-API-58b series closes this gap on the `RunOptions.env` tier across all five script-protocol-protected names × both API surfaces.

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/run.ts` (`runInternal` env merging at lines 661-664: `{ ...mergeEnv(globalEnv, localEnv, inheritedEnv), ...(snap.env ?? {}) }`) and `packages/loop-extender/src/execution.ts` (protocol-var overlay at lines 179-185: `{ ...env, LOOPX_BIN, LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT, LOOPX_WORKFLOW, LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR, LOOPX_TMPDIR }`) ALREADY conformed: the protocol-var overlay applies AFTER `snap.env` (which contains `RunOptions.env`) so any user-supplied `LOOPX_*` value — including NUL-containing values — is replaced before the merged env reaches `child_process.spawn`. The runtime's NUL-byte env-entry validator therefore never observes the bad value for any of the five script-protocol-protected names, and no spawn failure surfaces. Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **programmatic-api.test.ts: 576/576 PASS** (was 556, +20) — added 20 tests under the existing `SPEC: RunOptions.env LOOPX_* Silent Override` describe block. The block's pre-existing helpers (`makeIsolatedTmpdirParent` for SPEC §4.7 isolation) were extended into the block.
  - **T-API-58b (runPromise + LOOPX_WORKFLOW)** / **T-API-58c (run + LOOPX_WORKFLOW)**: 2 IDs × 2 runtimes = 4 tests. Bash fixture observes `LOOPX_WORKFLOW` into a marker + writes a `child-ran.txt` "spawned" marker. Driver passes `env: { LOOPX_WORKFLOW: "badvalue" }` under test-isolated TMPDIR parent. Asserts: (a) promise resolves / generator settles cleanly (no spawn-failure rejection — load-bearing — a buggy implementation that merged `RunOptions.env` BEFORE protocol injection would surface the NUL byte to spawn() and reject), (b) marker records `"ralph"` (real workflow name), NOT `"bad value"`, (c) stderr contains no `/exited with code/` or `/spawn/i` error, (d) stderr contains no `loopx_workflow.*(override|overrid|ignored|warning|notice)` warning (silent-override per SPEC §13 / §8.3), (e) workflow script ran exactly once (load-bearing — distinguishes from T-API-57's spawn-failure-no-script-ran outcome).
  - **T-API-58d (runPromise + LOOPX_TMPDIR)** / **T-API-58d2 (run + LOOPX_TMPDIR)**: 2 IDs × 2 runtimes = 4 tests. The dynamically-computed protocol-injection axis per SPEC §7.4 (value computed during pre-iteration, NOT derived from a static call-time identifier — structurally distinct from LOOPX_WORKFLOW). Bash fixture observes `LOOPX_TMPDIR` into a marker outside the tmpdir + performs an in-script `[ -d "$LOOPX_TMPDIR" ]` stat (during execution — SPEC §7.4 cleanup runs after the script, so a post-run stat would observe absence) + writes a `child-ran.txt` marker. Driver passes `env: { LOOPX_TMPDIR: "badvalue" }` under test-isolated TMPDIR parent. Asserts: (a) promise resolves / generator settles cleanly, (b) marker records a real absolute path under the test-isolated parent matching the SPEC §7.4 `loopx-XXX` mkdtemp naming convention, NOT `"bad value"`, (c) during-run stat marker records `"is-dir"` (proves the path points to a real loopx-created directory, not merely a substituted string — matching T-API-51a's rigor), (d) no spawn-failure error on stderr, (e) no `loopx_tmpdir.*(override|warning|notice)` regex on stderr, (f) workflow script ran. A buggy implementation that special-cased static-identifier protocol injection through one merge code path and dynamic-tmpdir injection through another would pass T-API-58b/58c yet fail T-API-58d/58d2.
  - **T-API-58e (runPromise — parameterized over LOOPX_BIN / LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT / LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR)** / **T-API-58e2 (run — same 3 names)**: 3 variants × 2 IDs × 2 runtimes = 12 tests. Parameterized hardening over the remaining three call-time-derived (but not workflow-identity-derived) names. Per-variant bash fixture observes the variant's name into a marker. Per-variant assertion on the real protocol value: LOOPX_BIN records an existing absolute path (`existsSync(observed) === true` — the resolved realpath of the running loopx binary), LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT records `realpathSync(project.dir)`, LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR records `join(projectRoot, ".loopx", "ralph")`. All five other assertions same as T-API-58b/c. Catches a buggy implementation that special-cased the two structurally-pinned names (LOOPX_WORKFLOW + LOOPX_TMPDIR) into one merge-order-correct code path while routing the remaining three through a separate, merge-order-broken path.
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions across tmpdir (569/569), env-vars + wfdir + loop-state + execution (311/311), signals (9/9), unit + harness + typecheck (172/172). Full programmatic-api.test.ts run: 576/576 in ~74s.

### ADR-0004 §9.5 / §8.3 / §13 (T-API-58a3/58a4 — RunOptions.envFile LOOPX_DELEGATED reaches child unchanged) — RESOLVED

SPEC §9.5 / §8.3 / §13 contract: `LOOPX_DELEGATED` is startup-reserved only on the loopx side and an ordinary non-protocol variable on the spawned-script side; the protocol-tier override that silently replaces script-protocol-protected `LOOPX_*` names (`LOOPX_BIN`, `LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR`, `LOOPX_TMPDIR`) does not apply to `LOOPX_DELEGATED`. The per-tier supply matrix has five env-supply tiers — inherited env (T-ENV-24a), global env file (T-ENV-24a2 — still pending in the P2 supplementary list), CLI local env file `-e` (T-ENV-24a3 — still pending), `RunOptions.env` (T-API-58a / T-API-58a2 — RESOLVED in the prior iteration), and programmatic `RunOptions.envFile` (this iteration). T-API-58a3/58a4 close the programmatic-`envFile` tier on both API surfaces, distinguishing `LOOPX_DELEGATED`'s startup-reserved-only classification from the script-protocol-protected names whose lower-tier values are silently overridden by protocol injection.

A buggy implementation that wired the no-protection behavior correctly on `RunOptions.env` (T-API-58a / 58a2), on the CLI `-e` path, on the global env file, and on inherited env, but used a separate code path for programmatic `RunOptions.envFile` that special-cased `LOOPX_DELEGATED` into the script-protocol-protected list (e.g., a duplicated env-merge table) would pass T-API-58a / 58a2 / T-ENV-24a and fail T-API-58a3/58a4.

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/run.ts` (`runInternal` env merging at lines 661-664: `{ ...mergeEnv(globalEnv, localEnv, inheritedEnv), ...(snap.env ?? {}) }`) and `packages/loop-extender/src/execution.ts` (protocol-var overlay at lines 179-185: `{ ...env, LOOPX_BIN, LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT, LOOPX_WORKFLOW, LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR, LOOPX_TMPDIR }`) ALREADY conformed: `LOOPX_DELEGATED` flows through the `localEnv` (envFile-loaded) → `mergeEnv` → spawn `env` chain unchanged because it is NOT in the protocol-var overlay list. Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **programmatic-api.test.ts: 556/556 PASS** (was 552, +4) — added 4 tests (2 IDs × 2 runtimes) extended into the existing `SPEC: RunOptions.env LOOPX_* Silent Override` describe block (which is now scoped to cover RunOptions.env + envFile both):
  - **T-API-58a3 (runPromise + RunOptions.envFile + LOOPX_DELEGATED)**: bash fixture observes `LOOPX_DELEGATED` into a marker. Local env file at `<test-tmp>/local.env` contains `LOOPX_DELEGATED=from-envfile\n`. Driver code scrubs `LOOPX_DELEGATED` from inherited env (`delete process.env.LOOPX_DELEGATED`) BEFORE calling `runPromise("ralph", { envFile, maxIterations: 1 })` — mirrors T-ENV-24a3's harness discipline. Asserts (a) promise resolves with one Output, (b) marker records `from-envfile` (load-bearing — the only tier supplying `LOOPX_DELEGATED` was the programmatic `envFile`, so the propagation must be byte-for-byte; a buggy implementation that scrubbed `LOOPX_DELEGATED` from the spawn env or applied protocol-tier override to it would surface `UNSET` and fail).
  - **T-API-58a4 (run + RunOptions.envFile + LOOPX_DELEGATED)**: same fixture and `delete` discipline, drained via `for await (const _ of run(...))`. Asserts (a) generator settles cleanly with one yield, (b) marker records `from-envfile`. Verifies a buggy implementation that wired the no-protection behavior correctly on the eager-snapshot `runPromise()` programmatic-envFile path while special-casing `LOOPX_DELEGATED` into the protected list under the lazy-snapshot `run()` programmatic-envFile path would pass T-API-58a3 and fail T-API-58a4.
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions — tmpdir (569/569), env-vars + wfdir + loop-state + execution (311/311), signals (9/9), unit + harness (158/158), typecheck OK. Full programmatic-api.test.ts run: 556/556 in ~72s.

### ADR-0004 §8.1 / §8.3 / §9.5 / §13 / §7.2 (T-API-58f/58f2 — RunOptions.envFile × NUL-protocol-name merge-order matrix on both API surfaces) — RESOLVED

SPEC §8.3 places loopx-injected protocol variables (`LOOPX_BIN`, `LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR`, `LOOPX_TMPDIR`) at the top precedence tier (tier 1) and silently overrides same-named values in any lower tier. SPEC §9.5 / §7.2 specify that runtime-level rejections of a child env entry (most reliably an embedded NUL byte in the value) "surface as child launch / spawn failures at spawn time" from "any env tier — the runtime does not distinguish tiers." T-API-58b/c/d/d2/e/e2 pinned the merge-order contract on the `RunOptions.env` tier (tier 2). The T-API-58f/58f2 series closes the same contract on the programmatic `RunOptions.envFile` tier (tier 3) across all five script-protocol-protected names × both API surfaces. Per SPEC §8.1: env-file values may contain embedded NUL bytes — the parser splits content on `\n` and reads from after the first `=` to end of line, with no NUL-byte filtering. The NUL byte therefore reaches `mergeEnv` unchanged from the envFile-loaded `localEnv`. The protocol-tier overlay in `execution.ts` (lines 179-185) applies AFTER the merged env is computed in `run.ts` (lines 661-664), so for the five script-protocol-protected names the user-supplied NUL value is replaced before the merged env reaches `child_process.spawn` — no spawn failure surfaces.

A buggy implementation that wired the protocol-tier-overlay-after-merge contract correctly on the `RunOptions.env` tier (passing T-API-58b..e2) but merged the programmatic envFile tier AFTER protocol injection (or used a separate merge code path that omitted the protocol-tier overlay) would surface a spawn-failure on the NUL byte and fail T-API-58f/58f2 axes (a)/(c)/(e).

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/run.ts` (`runInternal` env merging at lines 661-664: `{ ...mergeEnv(globalEnv, localEnv, inheritedEnv), ...(snap.env ?? {}) }`) and `packages/loop-extender/src/execution.ts` (protocol-var overlay at lines 179-185: `{ ...env, LOOPX_BIN, LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT, LOOPX_WORKFLOW, LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR, LOOPX_TMPDIR }`) ALREADY conformed: `mergeEnv` produces tiers 5→4→3 (where tier 3 includes envFile-loaded `localEnv`), `snap.env` overlays tier 2, protocol vars overlay tier 1 last, and the protocol-tier overlay's spread of fresh implementation-derived strings replaces any NUL-containing user-supplied value at the protocol-protected names BEFORE the merged env reaches `child_process.spawn`. Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **programmatic-api.test.ts: 596/596 PASS** (was 576, +20) — added 20 tests (10 unique it() bodies × 2 runtimes) under the existing `SPEC: RunOptions.env LOOPX_* Silent Override` describe block. Two parameterized `for` loops over five variants each (LOOPX_WORKFLOW / LOOPX_TMPDIR / LOOPX_BIN / LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT / LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR), one for runPromise() (T-API-58f) and one for run() (T-API-58f2). Each variant: writes `<NAME>=bad\x00value\n` to a local env file via `writeEnvFileRaw`, passes `envFile: <path>` to `runPromise()` / `run()` under a test-isolated TMPDIR parent, and asserts: (a) promise resolves / generator settles cleanly (no spawn-failure rejection — load-bearing — proves protocol-tier overlay replaced the NUL value before `spawn`), (b) marker records the real protocol value, NOT `"bad value"` — name-specific positive assertions: LOOPX_WORKFLOW marker == `"ralph"`; LOOPX_TMPDIR marker matches `/\/loopx-[^/]+$/` and starts with `realpathSync(tmpdirParent)`; LOOPX_BIN marker is an existing absolute path on disk; LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT marker == `realpathSync(project.dir)`; LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR marker == `join(projectRoot, ".loopx", "ralph")`, (c) for LOOPX_TMPDIR variant only, an in-script during-run `[ -d "$LOOPX_TMPDIR" ]` stat marker records `is-dir` (proves the path points to a real loopx-created directory, not merely a substituted string — matching T-API-51a/T-API-58d's rigor), (d) no spawn-failure error on stderr (no `/exited with code/` or `/spawn/i` regex match), (e) no override-warning on stderr (no `<name>.*(override|overrid|ignored|warning|notice)` regex match — silent-override per SPEC §13 / §8.3), (f) the workflow script ran exactly once (load-bearing — `child-ran.txt` marker exists; distinguishes from the spawn-failure-no-script-ran outcome that would result from a buggy merge order).
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions across tmpdir + env-vars + wfdir + loop-state + execution (880/880 across 5 e2e files), signals (9/9), unit + harness + typecheck (172/172). Full programmatic-api.test.ts run: 596/596 in ~77s.

### ADR-0004 §7.2 / §7.4 / §8.1 / §8.3 / §9.1 / §9.2 / §9.5 / §13 (T-API-58g/58g2 — programmatic global env-file × NUL-protocol-name merge-order matrix on both API surfaces) — RESOLVED

SPEC §8.3 places loopx-injected protocol variables (`LOOPX_BIN`, `LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR`, `LOOPX_TMPDIR`) at the top precedence tier (tier 1) and silently overrides same-named values in any lower tier. SPEC §9.5 / §7.2 specify that runtime-level rejections of a child env entry (most reliably an embedded NUL byte in the value) "surface as child launch / spawn failures at spawn time" from "any env tier — the runtime does not distinguish tiers." T-API-58b/c/d/d2/e/e2 pinned the merge-order contract on the `RunOptions.env` tier (tier 2). T-API-58f/58f2 closed the same contract on the programmatic local-env-file tier (tier 3 via `RunOptions.envFile`). The T-API-58g/58g2 series closes the global env-file tier (tier 4) on both programmatic API surfaces, completing the NUL × protocol-name merge-order matrix on the programmatic surface across all three lower tiers reachable via the programmatic API. SPEC §8.1: env-file values may contain embedded NUL bytes — the parser splits content on `\n` and reads from after the first `=` to end of line, with no NUL-byte filtering. The NUL byte therefore reaches `mergeEnv` unchanged from the global-env-file-loaded `globalEnv`. The protocol-tier overlay in `execution.ts` (lines 179-185) applies AFTER the merged env is computed in `run.ts` (lines 661-664), so for the five script-protocol-protected names the user-supplied NUL value is replaced before the merged env reaches `child_process.spawn` — no spawn failure surfaces.

A buggy implementation that wired the protocol-tier-overlay-after-merge contract correctly on the local-env-file tier (passing T-API-58f/58f2) but merged the global-env-file tier AFTER protocol injection on the programmatic surface (or used a separate merge code path that omitted the protocol-tier overlay for the global tier) would surface a spawn-failure on the NUL byte and fail T-API-58g/58g2 axes (a)/(d)/(f).

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/run.ts` (`runInternal` env merging at lines 661-664: `{ ...mergeEnv(globalEnv, localEnv, inheritedEnv), ...(snap.env ?? {}) }`) and `packages/loop-extender/src/execution.ts` (protocol-var overlay at lines 179-185: `{ ...env, LOOPX_BIN, LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT, LOOPX_WORKFLOW, LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR, LOOPX_TMPDIR }`) ALREADY conformed: `mergeEnv` produces tiers 5→4→3 (where tier 4 is the global-env-file-loaded `globalEnv`), `snap.env` overlays tier 2, protocol vars overlay tier 1 last, and the protocol-tier overlay's spread of fresh implementation-derived strings replaces any NUL-containing user-supplied value at the protocol-protected names BEFORE the merged env reaches `child_process.spawn`. Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **programmatic-api.test.ts: 616/616 PASS** (was 596, +20) — added 20 tests (10 unique it() bodies × 2 runtimes) under the existing `SPEC: RunOptions.env LOOPX_* Silent Override` describe block. Two parameterized `for` loops over five variants each (LOOPX_WORKFLOW / LOOPX_TMPDIR / LOOPX_BIN / LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT / LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR), one for runPromise() (T-API-58g) and one for run() (T-API-58g2). Each variant: provisions a writable XDG_CONFIG_HOME via `mkdtemp(join(osTmpdir(), "loopx-test-xdg-<id>-"))`, creates the `<xdg>/loopx/` subdirectory, writes `<NAME>=bad\x00value\n` raw to `<xdg>/loopx/env` via `writeEnvFileRaw`, then passes `XDG_CONFIG_HOME: xdgDir` (alongside `TMPDIR: tmpdirParent`) via `runAPIDriver` extraEnv so the spawned driver process inherits the test-isolated config home. No `envFile` is supplied — the global env file is the highest-precedence env-file tier reached, so a buggy implementation cannot mask its load by routing through the local-tier path. Asserts: (a) promise resolves / generator settles cleanly (no spawn-failure rejection — load-bearing — proves protocol-tier overlay replaced the NUL value before `spawn`), (b) marker records the real protocol value, NOT `"bad value"` — same per-variant positive assertions as T-API-58f: LOOPX_WORKFLOW == `"ralph"`; LOOPX_TMPDIR matches `/\/loopx-[^/]+$/` and starts with `realpathSync(tmpdirParent)`; LOOPX_BIN is an existing absolute path on disk; LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT == `realpathSync(project.dir)`; LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR == `join(projectRoot, ".loopx", "ralph")`, (c) for LOOPX_TMPDIR variant only, an in-script during-run `[ -d "$LOOPX_TMPDIR" ]` stat marker records `is-dir` (proves real loopx-created directory, not substituted string), (d) no spawn-failure error on stderr (no `/exited with code/`, no `/spawn/i`, no `/nul|\\x00/i`) — and no parser warning about NUL (per SPEC §8.1 the parser doesn't validate NUL in values), (e) no override-warning on stderr (no `<name>.*(override|overrid|ignored|warning|notice)` regex match — silent-override per SPEC §13 / §8.3), (f) workflow script ran exactly once (`child-ran.txt` marker exists). XDG_CONFIG_HOME directories are registered for cleanup via `cleanups.push`.
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions across tmpdir + env-vars + wfdir + loop-state + execution (880/880 across 5 e2e files), signals (9/9), unit + harness + typecheck (172/172). Full programmatic-api.test.ts run: 616/616 in ~80s.

### ADR-0004 §7.2 / §8.1 / §8.3 / §9.5 / §13 (T-ENV-28/28a/29/29a — CLI env-file × NUL-protocol-name merge-order matrix on both env-file tiers) — RESOLVED

SPEC §8.3 places loopx-injected protocol variables (`LOOPX_BIN`, `LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW`, `LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR`, `LOOPX_TMPDIR`) at the top precedence tier (tier 1) and silently overrides same-named values in any lower tier. SPEC §9.5 / §7.2 specify that runtime-level rejections of a child env entry (most reliably an embedded NUL byte in the value) "surface as child launch / spawn failures at spawn time" from "any env tier — the runtime does not distinguish tiers." Per SPEC §8.1: env-file values may contain embedded NUL bytes — the parser splits content on `\n` and reads from after the first `=` to end of line, with no NUL-byte filtering. T-API-58b/c/d/d2/e/e2 pinned the merge-order contract on the `RunOptions.env` tier (tier 2). T-API-58f/58f2 closed it on the programmatic local-env-file tier (tier 3 via `RunOptions.envFile`). T-API-58g/58g2 closed it on the programmatic global env-file tier (tier 4). T-ENV-28/28a/29/29a close the same contract on the CLI surface for both env-file tiers (tier 3 local `-e` and tier 4 global `<xdg>/loopx/env`) — completing the env-file × surface × name matrix.

A buggy implementation that wired the protocol-tier-overlay-after-merge contract correctly on the programmatic env-file paths (passing T-API-58f/f2/g/g2) but routed CLI env-file loading through a separate, merge-order-broken code path would pass T-API-58f/f2/g/g2 yet fail T-ENV-28/28a/29/29a.

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/run.ts` (`runInternal` env merging at lines 661-664: `{ ...mergeEnv(globalEnv, localEnv, inheritedEnv), ...(snap.env ?? {}) }`) and `packages/loop-extender/src/execution.ts` (protocol-var overlay at lines 179-185: `{ ...env, LOOPX_BIN, LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT, LOOPX_WORKFLOW, LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR, LOOPX_TMPDIR }`) ALREADY conformed: `mergeEnv` produces tiers 5→4→3 (where tier 3 is `-e`-loaded `localEnv` and tier 4 is the global-env-file-loaded `globalEnv`), `snap.env` overlays tier 2 (always undefined on the CLI surface), and the protocol-tier overlay overlays tier 1 last — replacing any NUL-containing user-supplied value at the protocol-protected names BEFORE the merged env reaches `child_process.spawn`. The CLI surface routes through the same `runInternal` code path as the programmatic surfaces, so no separate code path exists. Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **env-vars.test.ts: 116/116 PASS** (was 96, +20) — added 20 tests (10 unique it() bodies × 2 runtimes) under a new top-level `SPEC: CLI Env File LOOPX_* NUL Override` describe block. Each test runs under a test-isolated TMPDIR parent passed via `runCLI`'s extraEnv (no `process.env` mutation):
  - **T-ENV-28 (CLI -e + LOOPX_TMPDIR)**: 1 ID × 2 runtimes = 2 tests. Tests the dynamically-computed-protocol-injection axis on the CLI's local env-file tier. Writes `LOOPX_TMPDIR=bad\x00value\n` to a local env file via `writeEnvFileRaw`, runs `loopx run -e <local.env> -n 1 ralph` via `runCLI`. Asserts (a) exit code 0, (b) marker records a real absolute path under the test-isolated tmpdir parent matching `/\/loopx-[^/]+$/`, (c) during-run `[ -d "$LOOPX_TMPDIR" ]` stat marker records `is-dir`, (d) no spawn-failure error / NUL parser warning, (e) no override-warning, (f) workflow script ran.
  - **T-ENV-28a (i)–(iv) (CLI -e + 4 call-time-derived names)**: 4 variants × 2 runtimes = 8 tests. Parameterized over LOOPX_BIN / LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT / LOOPX_WORKFLOW / LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR. Same fixture / driver pattern as T-ENV-28 with per-variant positive marker assertions (LOOPX_BIN: existing absolute path; LOOPX_PROJECT_ROOT: `realpathSync(project.dir)`; LOOPX_WORKFLOW: `"ralph"`; LOOPX_WORKFLOW_DIR: `join(projectRoot, ".loopx", "ralph")`).
  - **T-ENV-29 (CLI global env file + LOOPX_TMPDIR)**: 1 ID × 2 runtimes = 2 tests. Provisions an isolated XDG_CONFIG_HOME via `mkdtemp`, writes the NUL-bearing line to `<xdg>/loopx/env` via `writeEnvFileRaw`, runs `loopx run -n 1 ralph` with `XDG_CONFIG_HOME=<xdg>` + `TMPDIR=<isolated>` in runCLI's extraEnv (no `envFile` so the global env file is the highest-precedence env-file tier reached — a buggy implementation cannot mask its load by routing through the local-tier path). Same five assertions as T-ENV-28.
  - **T-ENV-29a (i)–(iv) (CLI global env file + 4 call-time-derived names)**: 4 variants × 2 runtimes = 8 tests. Parameterized over the same four names as T-ENV-28a. Same fixture / driver pattern as T-ENV-29 with per-variant positive marker assertions.
- Test infrastructure added inline to env-vars.test.ts: `makeIsolatedTmpdirParent(label)` (under `tmpdir()` — TEST-SPEC §4.7), `makeIsolatedXdgConfigHome(label)` (parallel pattern for the global env-file tier), `assertObservedRealProtocolValue(name, observed, projectRoot, realTmpdirParent, tmpdirStatMarker)` (per-variant positive assertion dispatch), and `tmpdirStatBlock(name, marker)` (during-run-stat block injected into the bash workflow script for the LOOPX_TMPDIR variant only).
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions across programmatic-api (616/616) + tmpdir (569/569) + wfdir (40/40) + loop-state (96/96) + execution (79/79) + signals (9/9) + unit + harness (158/158), typecheck OK.

### ADR-0004 §8.1 / §8.3 / §9.1 / §9.5 (T-API-59 series — RunOptions.env / envFile do NOT redirect global env-file lookup) — RESOLVED

SPEC §8.1: "Global env file path resolution (`$XDG_CONFIG_HOME/loopx/env`, with the documented `HOME`-based fallback) reads `XDG_CONFIG_HOME` / `HOME` from the **inherited environment** on the same schedule." User-supplied `XDG_CONFIG_HOME` / `HOME` values via `RunOptions.env` (tier 2) or env files (tiers 3/4) reach the spawned child, but do not redirect WHERE loopx looks for its own global env file. T-API-59 series pins this contract across the {`RunOptions.env`, `RunOptions.envFile`, CLI `-e`} env-supply tiers × {`XDG_CONFIG_HOME`, `HOME`} fallback variables × {`runPromise()`, `run()`, CLI} surfaces.

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/env.ts:20-26` (`getGlobalEnvPath(envSnapshot?)`) ALREADY conformed: the path is resolved from `envSnapshot ?? process.env`, where `envSnapshot` is the eager inherited-env snapshot threaded down from `runPromise()` per SPEC §9.2. `RunOptions.env` (`snap.env`) is never consulted by `getGlobalEnvPath`. The `runInternal` path in `run.ts:634` calls `loadGlobalEnv(globalEnvPath)` BEFORE the merge step at line 661-664 that overlays `snap.env`, so `RunOptions.env` cannot influence which file `loadGlobalEnv` reads. Local env files at tier 3 are loaded at `run.ts:645` (also before the merge), but that load uses the path supplied via `snap.envFile` (the relative-or-absolute `envFile` path) — not any value INSIDE the file — so a `XDG_CONFIG_HOME=/fake` line within the local env file is loaded as a key-value entry that flows into tier 3 of the merge but never re-resolves the global path. Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

A buggy implementation that built the spawned-child environment first (merging inherited env + global env file + local env file + RunOptions.env) and *then* re-resolved the global env file path using the merged environment would pass any of the existing env tests (which all pin per-tier merge behavior) yet fail T-API-59 series — because the merged environment would have `XDG_CONFIG_HOME=/fake` (from RunOptions.env or local env file), and re-resolution would load the decoy `/fake/loopx/env` instead of the real `/real/loopx/env`.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **programmatic-api.test.ts: 632/632 PASS** (was 616, +16) — added 16 tests (8 unique it() bodies × 2 runtimes) under a new top-level `SPEC: RunOptions.env Does Not Affect Loopx's Own Lookups` describe block. Each test creates two `mkdtemp`-allocated config homes (`realXdg` containing `MARKER=real`, `fakeXdg` containing `MARKER=fake`), drives `runPromise` / `run` with `process.env.XDG_CONFIG_HOME = realXdg` (or `process.env.HOME = realHome` for HOME-fallback variants — also deletes XDG_CONFIG_HOME) via process.env mutation in driver code (matching T-API-71b/72b pattern), passes `env: { XDG_CONFIG_HOME: fakeXdg }` (or `envFile: <localPath>` containing `XDG_CONFIG_HOME=fakeXdg`), and asserts: (a) child observed XDG_CONFIG_HOME / HOME from `RunOptions.env` / local env file (the fake path — proves user-supplied value reached child via SPEC §8.3 tier 2 / tier 3 injection), (b) script-observed `MARKER === "real"` (proves loopx loaded global env file from inherited env, not from `RunOptions.env` / local env file).
  - **T-API-59 / 59a / 59b / 59c**: `runPromise()` × `run()` × `XDG_CONFIG_HOME` × `HOME` for the `RunOptions.env` tier. (4 it() bodies × 2 runtimes = 8 tests.)
  - **T-API-59d / 59e / 59h / 59i**: `runPromise()` × `run()` × `XDG_CONFIG_HOME` × `HOME` for the `RunOptions.envFile` tier (programmatic local env-file). (4 it() bodies × 2 runtimes = 8 tests.)
- **env-vars.test.ts: 120/120 PASS** (was 116, +4) — added 4 tests (2 unique it() bodies × 2 runtimes) under a new top-level `SPEC: CLI Env File Does Not Affect Loopx's Own Lookups` describe block. Each test creates two `mkdtemp`-allocated config homes, runs `loopx run -e <local.env> -n 1 ralph` via `runCLI` with `XDG_CONFIG_HOME=realXdg` (or `HOME=realHome` + `XDG_CONFIG_HOME=""` for the HOME-fallback variant — the empty-string XDG_CONFIG_HOME triggers the SPEC §8.1 HOME fallback at `env.ts:24` via the `||` falsy check) in runCLI's extraEnv. Local env file contains `XDG_CONFIG_HOME=fakeXdg` / `HOME=fakeHome`. Same assertions as the programmatic counterparts plus exit-code-0 check.
  - **T-API-59f / 59g**: CLI `-e` × `XDG_CONFIG_HOME` × `HOME`. (2 it() bodies × 2 runtimes = 4 tests.)
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions across tmpdir (569/569) + wfdir (40/40) + loop-state (96/96) + execution (79/79) + signals (9/9) + unit + harness (158/158), typecheck OK.

### ADR-0004 §7.4 / §8.3 / §9.1 / §9.5 (T-API-60/60a/60b/60c — RunOptions.env does NOT redirect tmpdir parent across both API surfaces × {TMPDIR, TEMP, TMP}) — RESOLVED

SPEC §7.4 / §9.5: loopx selects its tmpdir parent from `os.tmpdir()`, which itself reads `TMPDIR` / `TEMP` / `TMP` from the **inherited environment** (timing per SPEC §9.1 / §9.2 — eager call-site under `runPromise()`, lazy first-`next()` under `run()`). User-supplied values for those names via `RunOptions.env` (tier 2) reach the spawned child, but do not redirect the parent loopx selects for its own `mkdtemp(<parent>/loopx-)` call. T-API-60 series pins this contract on the API surface across {`runPromise()`, `run()`} × {`TMPDIR`, `TEMP`, `TMP`}, complementing T-TMP-29/29b/29c (in tmpdir.test.ts) which pin the same contract on the `runPromise()` surface only.

The implementation in `packages/loop-extender/src/run.ts` (`createTmpdir(parent)` invocation in `runLoop` reads `os.tmpdir()` from the inherited-env tier — never from `snap.env`) and `packages/loop-extender/src/tmpdir.ts` (`createTmpdir` itself uses the supplied parent verbatim) ALREADY conformed: the parent passed to `mkdtemp` is computed from `os.tmpdir()` at run-setup time using the runtime's read of inherited TMPDIR/TEMP/TMP — never from any merged or `snap.env`-overlaid env. `RunOptions.env` (`snap.env`) is overlaid on the per-spawn env passed to `child_process.spawn` AFTER the tmpdir-parent decision has already been made, so a user-supplied `RunOptions.env.TMPDIR` reaches the child but cannot influence loopx's own parent selection. Test-only iteration; no implementation changes required.

A buggy implementation that re-read `os.tmpdir()` after merging `RunOptions.env` into a working environment, or that special-cased one of the three branches of `os.tmpdir()` resolution (TMPDIR vs TEMP vs TMP) on one of the two surfaces, would pass T-TMP-29 yet fail one or more T-API-60 variants. The runtime-aware expected-parent assertion (via `getRuntimeOsTmpdir(runtime, envOverrides)`) handles the POSIX-vs-Windows split for the TEMP / TMP variants — on POSIX, `os.tmpdir()` only consults TMPDIR, so `LOOPX_TMPDIR` should land under the runtime's default `/tmp` (not `rightParent`); on Windows it should land under `rightParent`.

Now-passing tests (this iteration):
- **programmatic-api.test.ts: 640/640 PASS** (was 632, +8) — added 8 tests (4 unique it() bodies × 2 runtimes) under a new top-level `SPEC: RunOptions.env Does Not Affect Loopx's Tmpdir Parent` describe block:
  - **T-API-60**: `runPromise()` × TMPDIR. Passes `extraEnv: { TMPDIR: realParent }` to `runAPIDriver` (which strips the value from the spawned child's extraEnv and bakes a `process.env.TMPDIR = realParent` prefix into the driver code per the `tmpdirPrefix` mechanism in api-driver.ts), drives `runPromise("ralph", { env: { TMPDIR: fakeParent }, maxIterations: 1 })`. Bash fixture writes `$LOOPX_TMPDIR` and `$TMPDIR` to separate marker files. Asserts (a) `$TMPDIR` marker == fakeParent (RunOptions.env reaches child), (b) `dirname($LOOPX_TMPDIR marker)` == realParent (loopx selected its own tmpdir parent from inherited env, not from RunOptions.env). 1 ID × 2 runtimes = 2 tests.
  - **T-API-60a**: `run()` × TMPDIR. Generator-surface counterpart to T-API-60. Same fixture, driver code drives `for await (const _ of run("ralph", { env: { TMPDIR: fakeParent }, maxIterations: 1 })) {}`. Pins SPEC §9.1's lazy-snapshot timing on the run() surface — a buggy implementation that re-read RunOptions.env at first `next()` and merged it into the lazy process.env snapshot before computing `os.tmpdir()` would pass T-API-60 / T-TMP-29 but fail this test. 1 ID × 2 runtimes = 2 tests.
  - **T-API-60b**: `run()` × TEMP. Same generator-surface pattern. Driver code does `delete process.env.TMPDIR; delete process.env.TMP; process.env.TEMP = rightParent` before `run()`. Bash fixture observes `$LOOPX_TMPDIR` and `$TEMP`. Runtime-aware expected-parent assertion via `getRuntimeOsTmpdir(runtime, { TMPDIR: undefined, TMP: undefined, TEMP: rightParent })` — on POSIX runtimes, expected parent is whatever os.tmpdir() returns when only TEMP is set (typically /tmp); on Windows runtimes, expected parent is rightParent. Always asserts `$TEMP` marker == wrongParent (RunOptions.env reaches child). 1 ID × 2 runtimes = 2 tests.
  - **T-API-60c**: `run()` × TMP. Same runtime-aware pattern as T-API-60b for the TMP branch. Together with T-TMP-29/29b/29c (runPromise × all three), T-API-60a (run × TMPDIR), T-API-60b (run × TEMP), and this test, the matrix is closed across both run surfaces × all three variables. 1 ID × 2 runtimes = 2 tests.
- Test infrastructure added inline to programmatic-api.test.ts: `getRuntimeOsTmpdir(runtime, envOverrides)` (mirrored from tmpdir.test.ts — spawns a node/bun child with the given env and reads its os.tmpdir() return value), `makeIsolatedTmpdirParent(label)` (mkdtemp under osTmpdir, registered for cleanup), `makeNonexistentParent(label)` (`join(osTmpdir(), "loopx-test-${label}-fake-${randomUUID()}")` — used for the wrong-parent value passed via RunOptions.env, need not exist on disk because loopx must not consult it).
- Adjacent suites: zero regressions across tmpdir (569/569) + env-vars (120/120) + wfdir (40/40), typecheck OK. Full 4-suite run: 1369/1369 in ~215s.

The foundational T-API-65 series — T-API-65 / 65a / 65b / 65d (runPromise × pre-aborted signal beats missing env-file / invalid target / missing `.loopx/` / tmpdir-creation failure), T-API-65e (run() × invalid signal shape + missing envFile carve-out per SPEC §9.3 — does NOT enter abort pathway), and T-API-65k / 65l / 65m / 65n (run() generator-surface counterparts to 65 / 65a / 65b / 65d) — RESOLVED this iteration (9 unique IDs × 2 runtimes = 18 tests; test-only — existing implementation already conformed; see RESOLVED subsection above). T-API-65f / 65g (pre-aborted signal beats throwing later-option getter on both surfaces — pins SPEC §9.1 / §9.2 "signal first" read-order rule on the option-snapshot-error displacement axis) RESOLVED in earlier iteration (2 unique IDs × 2 runtimes = 4 tests; test-only — existing implementation already conformed; see RESOLVED subsection above). T-API-65a2 (non-string target argument variant — distinct from 65a's invalid-target-syntax branch; parameterized over `undefined` / `null` / `42` × both surfaces) RESOLVED in earlier iteration (3 variants × 2 surfaces × 2 runtimes = 12 tests; test-only — existing implementation already conformed; see RESOLVED subsection above). T-API-65h / 65i / 65j (target-resolution sub-paths: missing workflow / missing script in existing workflow / missing default `index` entry point — runPromise() surface) and T-API-65o (target-resolution sub-paths on `run()` generator surface — counterpart to 65h/65i/65j, parameterized over (a) missing workflow / (b) missing script / (c) missing default entry) RESOLVED this iteration (3 individual + 3 parameterized = 6 unique IDs × 2 runtimes = 12 tests; test-only — existing implementation already conformed; see RESOLVED subsection above). T-API-65c (unreadable local env file mode 000 — runPromise() surface, distinct from 65's missing-env-file branch; gated on `process.getuid() !== 0`) RESOLVED this iteration (1 unique ID × 2 runtimes = 2 tests; test-only — existing implementation already conformed; see RESOLVED subsection above). Remaining T-API-65 sub-IDs still need authoring: T-API-65p / 65q RESOLVED this iteration (16-variant exhaustive option-snapshot matrix on `runPromise()` and `run()` — extends 65f/65g coverage; see RESOLVED subsection above), T-API-65r RESOLVED this iteration (unreadable global env file × both surfaces — gated on `process.getuid() !== 0`; see RESOLVED subsection above), T-API-65s RESOLVED in earlier iteration (sibling-validation discovery failure × both surfaces — see RESOLVED subsection above), T-API-65t RESOLVED this iteration (name-restriction discovery failure × both surfaces × 2 fixtures — see RESOLVED subsection above), T-API-65u / 65u2 / 65u3 (reentrant duck-signal abort wins over later pre-iteration failure × 2 disjuncts × 2 variants × both surfaces), T-API-65v / 65w RESOLVED this iteration (invalid options wrapper carrying aborted signal does NOT enter abort pathway — carve-out parity with 65e on both surfaces; see RESOLVED subsection above), T-API-65x / 65y (pre-aborted signal does not compete with workflow-level version warning × both surfaces). T-API-67..69u (generator lifecycle, promise rejection) still need authoring.
- **T-API-70..74c** — 15 remaining programmatic API tests.
- **T-INST-110..120e** — Auto-install ADR-0004 (~100 tests): `npm install`, `--no-install`, `.gitignore` safeguard, malformed `package.json` skip, npm-install failure handling, signals during npm install, no-rollback semantics, `-y` interaction, environment isolation, streaming passthrough, npm-only manager selection.
- **T-INST-55f..55zj** — symlink source validation (~40 tests).
- **T-INST-40f, T-INST-44a..44f** — `--no-install` CLI parsing (duplicate rejection, help interaction, no short alias).
- **T-INST-DASHDASH-01..04** — `--` rejection on install.
- **T-INST-42m, 42n** — install help-text content pins.

RESOLVED this iteration: T-EXEC-03b/03c (cd cwd-isolation across goto + loop reset), T-EXEC-07a/07b (Bash invocation: no executable bit + absolute /bin/bash), T-EXEC-13c..13m (CJS-rejection matrix: 11 tests covering `require` / `module.exports` / `exports.foo` × `.js`/`.ts`/`.tsx`/`.jsx`), T-EXEC-16c/16d (`process.chdir()` cwd-isolation across goto + loop reset).

## Pre-existing failures (not ADR-0004)

- **T-INST-GLOBAL-01a** — `[Bun] full global install lifecycle with import 'loopx'` fails with "Module not found … /loop-extender/bin.js". Pre-existing issue with Bun's resolution at the global-install layout. Unrelated to ADR-0004; confirmed by reproducing the failure on baseline (pre-change) source. Should be triaged separately.
- **Bun-under-full-parallelism failures** — Running the entire `npm run test` matrix in full parallelism surfaces ~32 additional `[Bun]`-runtime failures across module-resolution / wfdir / execution / install test files. Confirmed pre-existing via `git stash`: the same 32 failures reproduce with this iteration's changes stashed, and they do NOT reproduce when running the e2e suites alone (e2e-only run shows 1 failure: T-INST-GLOBAL-01a above). Likely a parallelism / isolation issue in the test harness or Bun's loader behavior under concurrent test workers; unrelated to ADR-0004 and out of scope for this work.

## Notes

- `.loopx/.iteration.tmp` and `.loopx/ralph/.tmp/` appear in `git status` — left by prior loopx runs, not part of this work. Not tracked.
